### 21. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `d99afc63-7b10-8c88-fa72-35633207024f`

```sql
SELECT bddcria.InstrumentID
	 , bddcria.Instrument
	 , bddcria.InstrumentTypeID
	 , bddcria.InstrumentType
	 , bddcria.Region
	 , bddcria.Club
	 , bddcria.FullDate
	 , bddcria.DateID
	 , bddcria.[FTD Year]
	 , bddcria.VolumeOnOpen
	 , bddcria.VolumeOnClose
	 , bddcria.RollOverFee
	 , ISNULL(bddcria.FullCommissions,0) + ISNULL(bddcria.TradingFees,0) AS FullCommissions
	 , bddcria.Commissions
	 , bddcria.IsValidCustomer
	 , bddcria.Regulation
	 , bddcria.IsSettled
	 , bddcria.RollOverFee_SDRT
	 , bddcria.TradingFees
	 , bddcria.IsDLTUser
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg bddcria
WHERE bddcria.DateID >= 20240101
```

### 22. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `df1c9c77-bf32-ae69-4f5e-051e52322163`

```sql
SELECT q0.CalendarYearMonth
	  ,q0.FullDate
	  ,q0.Region
	  ,q0.InstrumentType
	  ,q0.Club
	  ,q0.ExchangeCountry
	  ,q0.IsSettled
	  ,SUM(q0.Volume       ) Volume
	  ,SUM(q0.Transactions ) Transactions
	  ,SUM(q0.Commission   ) Commission
	  ,SUM(q0.RolloverFee  ) RolloverFee 
FROM 
(
SELECT dd.CalendarYearMonth
      ,MIN(dd.FullDate) FullDate
      ,dc1.MarketingRegionManualName Region
	  ,di.InstrumentType
	  ,dpl.Name Club
      ,CASE WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Bolsa De Madrid','Euronext Lisbon') THEN 'Spain'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'Borsa Italiana' THEN 'Italian'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'LSE' THEN 'UK'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Chicago Board Options Exchange','Extended Hours Trading','NYSE','Nasdaq','OTC Markets Stock Exchange') THEN 'USA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Copenhagen Stock Exchange','Euronext Lisbon','Helsinki Stock Exchange','Oslo Stock Exchange','Stockholm  Stock Exchange') THEN 'Nordics'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Euronext Brussels','Euronext Paris') THEN 'French'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('FRA','SIX') THEN 'German'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Hong Kong Exchanges') THEN 'SEA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Sydney') THEN 'Australia'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Tadawul') THEN 'Arabic'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('CFD','Digital Currency','Commodity','FX') THEN 'No Exchange'
			ELSE 'Others' END ExchangeCountry
	  ,dp.IsSettled
	  ,SUM(CONVERT(BIGINT,dp.VolumeOnClose)) Volume
      ,COUNT(*) Transactions
	  ,0 Commission
	  ,0 RolloverFee
FROM [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Position] dp WITH (NOLOCK)
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Instrument] di WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dp.InstrumentID = di.InstrumentID
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Customer] dc WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dp.CID = dc.RealCID
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Country] dc1 WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dc.CountryID = dc1.CountryID
INNER JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Date dd WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dp.CloseDateID = dd.DateKey
INNER JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_PlayerLevel dpl WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dc.PlayerLevelID = dpl.PlayerLevelID
WHERE dd.DateKey >= 20230101
AND IsValidCustomer = 1
GROUP BY dc1.MarketingRegionManualName 
      ,dd.CalendarYearMonth
	  ,di.InstrumentType
	  ,dpl.Name 
      ,CASE WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Bolsa De Madrid','Euronext Lisbon') THEN 'Spain'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'Borsa Italiana' THEN 'Italian'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'LSE' THEN 'UK'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Chicago Board Options Exchange','Extended Hours Trading','NYSE','Nasdaq','OTC Markets Stock Exchange') THEN 'USA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Copenhagen Stock Exchange','Euronext Lisbon','Helsinki Stock Exchange','Oslo Stock Exchange','Stockholm  Stock Exchange') THEN 'Nordics'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Euronext Brussels','Euronext Paris') THEN 'French'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('FRA','SIX') THEN 'German'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Hong Kong Exchanges') THEN 'SEA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Sydney') THEN 'Australia'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Tadawul') THEN 'Arabic'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('CFD','Digital Currency','Commodity','FX') THEN 'No Exchange'
			ELSE 'Others' END
	  ,dp.IsSettled
UNION all
SELECT dd.CalendarYearMonth
      ,MIN(dd.FullDate) FullDate
      ,dc1.MarketingRegionManualName Region
	  ,di.InstrumentType
	  ,dpl.Name Club
      ,CASE WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Bolsa De Madrid','Euronext Lisbon') THEN 'Spain'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'Borsa Italiana' THEN 'Italian'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'LSE' THEN 'UK'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Chicago Board Options Exchange','Extended Hours Trading','NYSE','Nasdaq','OTC Markets Stock Exchange') THEN 'USA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Copenhagen Stock Exchange','Euronext Lisbon','Helsinki Stock Exchange','Oslo Stock Exchange','Stockholm  Stock Exchange') THEN 'Nordics'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Euronext Brussels','Euronext Paris') THEN 'French'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('FRA','SIX') THEN 'German'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Hong Kong Exchanges') THEN 'SEA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Sydney') THEN 'Australia'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Tadawul') THEN 'Arabic'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('CFD','Digital Currency','Commodity','FX') THEN 'No Exchange'
			ELSE 'Others' END ExchangeCountry
	  ,dp.IsSettled
	  ,SUM(CONVERT(BIGINT,dp.Volume)) Volume
      ,COUNT(CASE WHEN ISNULL(dp.IsPartialCloseChild,0) = 0 THEN dp.PositionID END) Transactions
	  ,0 Commission
	  ,0 RolloverFee
FROM [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Position] dp WITH (NOLOCK)
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Instrument] di WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dp.InstrumentID = di.InstrumentID
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Customer] dc WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dp.CID = dc.RealCID
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Country] dc1 WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dc.CountryID = dc1.CountryID
INNER JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Date dd WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dp.OpenDateID = dd.DateKey
INNER JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_PlayerLevel dpl WITH (NOLOCK)
ON dc.PlayerLevelID = dpl.PlayerLevelID
WHERE dd.DateKey >=20230101
AND IsValidCustomer = 1
GROUP BY dc1.MarketingRegionManualName
      ,dd.CalendarYearMonth
	  ,di.InstrumentType
	  ,dpl.Name
      ,CASE WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Bolsa De Madrid','Euronext Lisbon') THEN 'Spain'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'Borsa Italiana' THEN 'Italian'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'LSE' THEN 'UK'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Chicago Board Options Exchange','Extended Hours Trading','NYSE','Nasdaq','OTC Markets Stock Exchange') THEN 'USA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Copenhagen Stock Exchange','Euronext Lisbon','Helsinki Stock Exchange','Oslo Stock Exchange','Stockholm  Stock Exchange') THEN 'Nordics'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Euronext Brussels','Euronext Paris') THEN 'French'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('FRA','SIX') THEN 'German'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Hong Kong Exchanges') THEN 'SEA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Sydney') THEN 'Australia'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Tadawul') THEN 'Arabic'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('CFD','Digital Currency','Commodity','FX') THEN 'No Exchange'
			ELSE 'Others' END
	  ,dp.IsSettled
UNION ALL
SELECT dd.CalendarYearMonth
      ,MIN(dd.FullDate) FullDate
	  ,bddcria.Region 
	  ,bddcria.InstrumentType
	  ,bddcria.Club
	  ,CASE WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Bolsa De Madrid','Euronext Lisbon') THEN 'Spain'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'Borsa Italiana' THEN 'Italian'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'LSE' THEN 'UK'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Chicago Board Options Exchange','Extended Hours Trading','NYSE','Nasdaq','OTC Markets Stock Exchange') THEN 'USA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Copenhagen Stock Exchange','Euronext Lisbon','Helsinki Stock Exchange','Oslo Stock Exchange','Stockholm  Stock Exchange') THEN 'Nordics'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Euronext Brussels','Euronext Paris') THEN 'French'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('FRA','SIX') THEN 'German'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Hong Kong Exchanges') THEN 'SEA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Sydney') THEN 'Australia'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Tadawul') THEN 'Arabic'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('CFD','Digital Currency','Commodity','FX') THEN 'No Exchange'
			ELSE 'Others' END ExchangeCounty
	  ,bddcria.IsSettled
	  ,0 Volume
	  ,0 Transactions
	  ,SUM(bddcria.FullCommissions) Commission
	  ,SUM(bddcria.RollOverFee) RolloverFee
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg bddcria
INNER JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Date dd WITH (NOLOCK)
ON bddcria.DateID = dd.DateKey
INNER JOIN [DWH_dbo].[Dim_Instrument] di WITH (NOLOCK)
ON bddcria.InstrumentID = di.InstrumentID
WHERE dd.DateKey >=20230101
AND bddcria.IsValidCustomer = 1
GROUP BY dd.CalendarYearMonth
	  ,bddcria.Region 
	  ,bddcria.InstrumentType
	  ,bddcria.Club
	  ,CASE WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Bolsa De Madrid','Euronext Lisbon') THEN 'Spain'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'Borsa Italiana' THEN 'Italian'
			WHEN di.Exchange = 'LSE' THEN 'UK'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Chicago Board Options Exchange','Extended Hours Trading','NYSE','Nasdaq','OTC Markets Stock Exchange') THEN 'USA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Copenhagen Stock Exchange','Euronext Lisbon','Helsinki Stock Exchange','Oslo Stock Exchange','Stockholm  Stock Exchange') THEN 'Nordics'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Euronext Brussels','Euronext Paris') THEN 'French'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('FRA','SIX') THEN 'German'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Hong Kong Exchanges') THEN 'SEA'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Sydney') THEN 'Australia'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('Tadawul') THEN 'Arabic'
			WHEN di.Exchange IN ('CFD','Digital Currency','Commodity','FX') THEN 'No Exchange'
			ELSE 'Others' END
	  ,bddcria.IsSettled
	  )q0
	  GROUP BY q0.CalendarYearMonth
	  ,q0.FullDate
	  ,q0.Region
	  ,q0.InstrumentType
	  ,q0.Club
	  ,q0.ExchangeCountry
	  ,q0.IsSettled
```

### 23. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `e0fd4602-b5a7-0a50-0536-dad7138b068c`

```sql
SELECT  
    a.[Period],
    a.InstrumentType,
    a.IsSettled,
    a.Region,
    a.Club,
    a.[FTD Year],
    a.Metric,
    a.DateID,
    CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), a.DateID), 112) AS Date,
    SUM(a.Amount) AS Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
        'SameDay8Weeks' AS [Period],
        InstrumentType,
        IsSettled,
        Region,
        Club,
        [FTD Year],
        Metric,
        Amount,
        DateID,
        CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), DateID), 112) AS Date
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT 
            InstrumentType,
            IsSettled,
            Region,
            Club,
            [FTD Year],
            DateID,
            SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
            SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
            SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
            SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
            SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
            SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
            SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
            SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
            SUM(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
        FROM 
        (
            SELECT ia.*
            FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg ia
            WHERE 
                IsValidCustomer = 1
                AND ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, ia.FullDate) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1 
                    = ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, GETDATE() - 1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1
                AND DATEDIFF(WEEK, ia.FullDate, GETDATE() - 1) <= 8
        ) AS Filtered
        GROUP BY 
            InstrumentType,
            IsSettled,
            Region,
            Club,
            [FTD Year],
            Filtered.DateID
    ) AS Aggregated
    UNPIVOT (
        Amount FOR Metric IN (
            Commissions,
            FullCommissions,
            RollOverFee,
            TicketFee,
            TicketFeeByPercent,
            AdminFee,
            SpotAdjustFee,
            Volume,
            Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
        )
    ) AS unpvt
) a
GROUP BY 
    a.[Period],  
    a.Metric, 
    a.InstrumentType, 
    a.IsSettled, 
    a.Region, 
    a.Club, 
    a.[FTD Year], 
    a.DateID, 
    CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), a.DateID), 112)
```

### 24. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `e1a3665a-696d-0b0d-a0d6-fdf0cdbcc15f`

```sql
SELECT
	   a.Metric
	 , a.IncomeCategory
	 , a.InstrumentTypeID
	 , a.IsSettled
	 , a.Region
	 , sum(a.Amount) AS Amount
	, di.InstrumentType
	, CASE WHEN a.IsSettled = 1 THEN 'Real' 
			WHEN a.IsSettled = 0 THEN 'CFD'
	  ELSE 'NA' 
	  END AS CFD_Real
  , YEAR(a.Date) AS [Year]
  , YEAR(a.Date) * 100 + DATEPART(qq, a.Date) AS YearQuarter
  , convert(varchar(6),a.Date,112) AS YearMonth
  , dd.ISOYearAndWeekNumber AS YearWeek
  , dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start AS DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start
  , DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1) AS WeekDiff
  , CASE WHEN DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1) <= 7 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsLast8Weeks
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsCurrentYear
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPreviousYear
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsCurrentMonth
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPreviousMonth
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE)) AND getdate()-1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsCurrentWeek
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(WEEK, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) AND DATEADD(DAY, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPreviousWeek
  , CASE WHEN dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start = (DATEPART(WEEKDAY,getdate()-1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7 + 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsSameWeekDayAsReference
FROM 
(
SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'FullCommission' AS Metric
	  , 'OpenClosePosition' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.FullCommissions) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'TicketFee' AS Metric
	  , 'OpenClosePosition' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.TicketFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) 
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'TicketFeeByPercent' AS Metric
	  , 'OpenClosePosition' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.TicketFeeByPercent) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) 
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'RollOverFee' AS Metric
	  , 'Overnight' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.RollOverFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'AdminFee' AS Metric
	  , 'Overnight' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.AdminFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) 
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'SpotAdjustFee' AS Metric
	  , 'Overnight' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.SpotAdjustFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'Volume' AS Metric
	  , 'NA' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (ISNULL(frfc.VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(frfc.VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]	  


UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'InvestedAmountOpen' AS Metric
	  , 'NA' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.InvestedAmountOpen) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'CountUU' AS Metric
	  , 'NA' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.CountUU) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

) a
	JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT InstrumentTypeID, InstrumentType FROM DWH_dbo.Dim_Instrument) di
		ON a.InstrumentTypeID = di.InstrumentTypeID
	JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Date dd
		ON a.DateID = dd.DateKey
GROUP BY 
	a.Metric
  , a.IncomeCategory
  , a.InstrumentTypeID
  , a.IsSettled
  , di.InstrumentType
  , a.Region
  , CASE WHEN a.IsSettled = 1 THEN 'Real' WHEN a.IsSettled = 0 THEN 'CFD' ELSE 'NA'  END 
  ,	YEAR(a.Date) 
  , YEAR(a.Date) * 100 + DATEPART(qq, a.Date) 
  , convert(varchar(6),a.Date,112) 
  , dd.ISOYearAndWeekNumber 
  , dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start 
  , DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1)
  , CASE WHEN DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1) <= 7 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE)) AND getdate()-1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(WEEK, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) AND DATEADD(DAY, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start = (DATEPART(WEEKDAY,getdate()-1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7 + 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
```

### 25. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `ed9176db-93c5-2651-3d0d-b6bd4f4469e8`

```sql
SELECT
	   a.Metric
	 , a.IncomeCategory
	 , a.InstrumentTypeID
	 , a.IsSettled
	 , sum(a.Amount) AS Amount
	, di.InstrumentType
	, CASE WHEN a.IsSettled = 1 THEN 'Real' 
			WHEN a.IsSettled = 0 THEN 'CFD'
	  ELSE 'NA' 
	  END AS CFD_Real
  , YEAR(a.Date) AS [Year]
  , YEAR(a.Date) * 100 + DATEPART(qq, a.Date) AS YearQuarter
  , convert(varchar(6),a.Date,112) AS YearMonth
  , dd.ISOYearAndWeekNumber AS YearWeek
  , dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start AS DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start
  , DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1) AS WeekDiff
  , CASE WHEN DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1) <= 7 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsLast8Weeks
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsCurrentYear
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPreviousYear
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsCurrentMonth
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPreviousMonth
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE)) AND getdate()-1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsCurrentWeek
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(WEEK, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) AND DATEADD(DAY, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPreviousWeek
  , CASE WHEN dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start = (DATEPART(WEEKDAY,getdate()-1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7 + 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsSameWeekDayAsReference
FROM 
(
SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'FullCommission' AS Metric
	  , 'OpenClosePosition' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.FullCommissions) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'TicketFee' AS Metric
	  , 'OpenClosePosition' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.TicketFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) 
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'TicketFeeByPercent' AS Metric
	  , 'OpenClosePosition' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.TicketFeeByPercent) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) 
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'RollOverFee' AS Metric
	  , 'Overnight' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.RollOverFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'AdminFee' AS Metric
	  , 'Overnight' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.AdminFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112) 
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'SpotAdjustFee' AS Metric
	  , 'Overnight' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.SpotAdjustFee) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'Volume' AS Metric
	  , 'NA' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (ISNULL(frfc.VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(frfc.VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]	  


UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'InvestedAmountOpen' AS Metric
	  , 'NA' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.InvestedAmountOpen) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

UNION ALL 

SELECT CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  AS [Date]
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , 'CountUU' AS Metric
	  , 'NA' AS IncomeCategory
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , ISNULL(frfc.IsSettled,0) AS IsSettled
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]
	  , SUM (frfc.CountUU) AS Amount
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg frfc
WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST (FORMAT (CAST (DATEFROMPARTS (YEAR (getdate()-1)-1, 1, 1) AS DATE), 'yyyyMMdd') AS INT) and CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
GROUP BY 
		frfc.DateID 
	  , frfc.DateID
	  , frfc.InstrumentTypeID
	  , frfc.IsSettled
	  , CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), frfc.DateID), 112)  
	  , frfc.Region
	  , frfc.Club
	  , frfc.[FTD Year]

) a
	JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT InstrumentTypeID, InstrumentType FROM DWH_dbo.Dim_Instrument) di
		ON a.InstrumentTypeID = di.InstrumentTypeID
	JOIN DWH_dbo.Dim_Date dd
		ON a.DateID = dd.DateKey
GROUP BY 
	a.Metric
  , a.IncomeCategory
  , a.InstrumentTypeID
  , a.IsSettled
  , di.InstrumentType
  , CASE WHEN a.IsSettled = 1 THEN 'Real' WHEN a.IsSettled = 0 THEN 'CFD' ELSE 'NA'  END 
  ,	YEAR(a.Date) 
  , YEAR(a.Date) * 100 + DATEPART(qq, a.Date) 
  , convert(varchar(6),a.Date,112) 
  , dd.ISOYearAndWeekNumber 
  , dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start 
  , DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1)
  , CASE WHEN DATEDIFF (WEEK, a.Date, getdate()-1) <= 7 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
  , CASE WHEN YEAR(a.Date) = year (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN Month(a.Date) = Month (getdate()-1) - 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE)) AND getdate()-1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN a.Date BETWEEN DATEADD(WEEK, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) AND DATEADD(DAY, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END 
  , CASE WHEN dd.DayNumberOfWeek_Sun_Start = (DATEPART(WEEKDAY,getdate()-1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7 + 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
```

### 26. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f353fe36-47d4-d730-0658-d18b87c4584c`

```sql
SELECT  
    a.[Period],
    a.InstrumentType,
    a.IsSettled,
    a.Region,
    a.Club,
    a.[FTD Year],
    a.Metric,
    a.DateID,
    CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), a.DateID), 112) AS Date,
    SUM(a.Amount) AS Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
        'SameDay8Weeks' AS [Period],
        InstrumentType,
        IsSettled,
        Region,
        Club,
        [FTD Year],
        Metric,
        Amount,
        DateID,
        CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), DateID), 112) AS Date
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT 
            InstrumentType,
            IsSettled,
            Region,
            Club,
            [FTD Year],
            DateID,
            SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
            SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
            SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
            SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
            SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
            SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
            SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
            SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
            SUM(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
        FROM 
        (
            SELECT ia.*
            FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg ia
            WHERE 
                IsValidCustomer = 1
                AND ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, ia.FullDate) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1 
                    = ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, GETDATE() - 1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1
                AND DATEDIFF(WEEK, ia.FullDate, GETDATE() - 1) <= 8
        ) AS Filtered
        GROUP BY 
            InstrumentType,
            IsSettled,
            Region,
            Club,
            [FTD Year],
            Filtered.DateID
    ) AS Aggregated
    UNPIVOT (
        Amount FOR Metric IN (
            Commissions,
            FullCommissions,
            RollOverFee,
            TicketFee,
            TicketFeeByPercent,
            AdminFee,
            SpotAdjustFee,
            Volume,
            Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
        )
    ) AS unpvt
) a
GROUP BY 
    a.[Period],  
    a.Metric, 
    a.InstrumentType, 
    a.IsSettled, 
    a.Region, 
    a.Club, 
    a.[FTD Year], 
    a.DateID, 
    CONVERT(DATE, CONVERT(VARCHAR(8), a.DateID), 112)
```

### 27. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `f711bbe9-f2ad-756e-4388-139b6ec6cbca`

```sql
--- yesterday

SELECT 
	'Yesterday' AS [Period],
	InstrumentType,
	IsSettled,
	Region,
	Club,
	[FTD Year],
    Metric,
    Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
		InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year],
        SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
        SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
        SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
        SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
        SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
        SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
        SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
        SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
		sum(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT *
        FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
        WHERE 
            IsValidCustomer = 1
            AND DateID = CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)
    ) AS Filtered
    GROUP BY InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year]
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
    Amount FOR Metric IN (
        Commissions,
        FullCommissions,
        RollOverFee,
        TicketFee,
        TicketFeeByPercent,
        AdminFee,
        SpotAdjustFee,
		Volume,
		Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
    )
) AS unpvt

--- This Month

UNION all 

-- DECLARE getdate()-1 DATE = getdate()-1

SELECT 
	'CurrentMonth' AS [Period],
	InstrumentType,
	IsSettled,
	Region,
	Club,
	[FTD Year],
    Metric,
    Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
		InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year],
        SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
        SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
        SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
        SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
        SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
        SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
        SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
        SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
		sum(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT *
        FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
        WHERE 
            IsValidCustomer = 1
            AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST(DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, getdate()-1), 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
    ) AS Filtered
    GROUP BY InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year]
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
    Amount FOR Metric IN (
        Commissions,
        FullCommissions,
        RollOverFee,
        TicketFee,
        TicketFeeByPercent,
        AdminFee,
        SpotAdjustFee,
		Volume,
		Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
    )
) AS unpvt

--- Last Month

	'PreviousMonthSameTime' AS [Period],

    FROM

        SELECT *
        FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg

            IsValidCustomer = 1
            AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST( DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, getdate()-1) - 1, 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(dateadd(MONTH,-1,getdate()-1)  AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
    ) AS Filtered
    GROUP BY InstrumentType,

SELECT 
	'CurrentWeek' AS [Period],
	InstrumentType,
	IsSettled,
	Region,
	Club,
	[FTD Year],
    Metric,
    Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
		InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year],
        SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
        SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
        SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
        SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
        SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
        SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
        SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
        SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
		sum(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT *
        FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
        WHERE 
            IsValidCustomer = 1
            AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST(DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)  AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
    ) AS Filtered
    GROUP BY InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year]
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
    Amount FOR Metric IN (
        Commissions,
        FullCommissions,
        RollOverFee,
        TicketFee,
        TicketFeeByPercent,
        AdminFee,
        SpotAdjustFee,
		Volume,
		Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
    )
) AS unpvt

union all 



-- DECLARE getdate()-1 DATE = getdate()-1

SELECT 
	'PreviousWeekSameTime' AS [Period],
	InstrumentType,
	IsSettled,
	Region,
	Club,
	[FTD Year],
    Metric,
    Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
		InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year],
        SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
        SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
        SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
        SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
        SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
        SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
        SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
        SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
		sum(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT *
        FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
        WHERE 
            IsValidCustomer = 1
            AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST(dateadd (WEEK, -1, DATEADD(DAY, 1 - DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1), getdate()-1)) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)  AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(dateadd(WEEK, -1,getdate()-1) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
    ) AS Filtered
    GROUP BY InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year]
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
    Amount FOR Metric IN (
        Commissions,
        FullCommissions,
        RollOverFee,
        TicketFee,
        TicketFeeByPercent,
        AdminFee,
        SpotAdjustFee,
		Volume,
		Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
    )
) AS unpvt

UNION ALL 



-- DECLARE getdate()-1 DATE = getdate()-1

SELECT 
	'CurrentQuarter' AS [Period],
	InstrumentType,
	IsSettled,
	Region,
	Club,
	[FTD Year],
    Metric,
    Amount
FROM 
(
    SELECT 
		InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year],
        SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
        SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
        SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
        SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
        SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
        SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
        SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
        SUM(ISNULL(VolumeOnOpen,0) + ISNULL(VolumeOnClose,0)) AS Volume,
		sum(Filtered.InvestedAmountOpen) AS InvestedAmountOpen
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT *
        FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
        WHERE 
            IsValidCustomer = 1
            AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST( DATEADD(qq, DATEDIFF(qq, 0, getdate()-1), 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)  AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
    ) AS Filtered
    GROUP BY InstrumentType,
		IsSettled,
		Region,
		Club,
		[FTD Year]
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
    Amount FOR Metric IN (
        Commissions,
        FullCommissions,
        RollOverFee,
        TicketFee,
        TicketFeeByPercent,
        AdminFee,
        SpotAdjustFee,
		Volume,
		Aggregated.InvestedAmountOpen
    )
) AS unpvt

```

### 28. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `fa7fee7f-708c-6aab-cd6b-5e3a1665995d`

```sql
select InstrumentID, Instrument, Regulation,
	EOMONTH(FullDate) AS EoM,
	sum(VolumeOnOpen) AS VolumeOnOpen, 
	sum(VolumeOnClose) AS VolumeOnClose,  
	sum(VolumeOnOpen) + sum(VolumeOnClose) AS TotalVolume
from BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
where  DateID>= 20250101
AND InstrumentTypeID = 10
AND Regulation IN ('FinCEN+FINRA','FinCEN')
AND IsValidCustomer=1
GROUP BY InstrumentID, Instrument, Regulation,
	EOMONTH(FullDate)
--ORDER BY EOMONTH(FullDate), InstrumentID
```

### 29. Custom SQL Query

- Tableau id: `ff83b4c9-b120-ee8a-ad73-346bca9810c3`

```sql
SELECT 
	'Yesterday' AS [Period],
	Instrument,
	InstrumentType,
	Metric,
	Amount
FROM 
(
	SELECT 
		Instrument,
		InstrumentType,
		SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
		SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
		SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
		SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
		SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
		SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
		SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
		SUM(VolumeOnOpen) AS VolumeOnOpen,
		SUM(VolumeOnClose) AS VolumeOnClose
	FROM 
	(
		SELECT Instrument, InstrumentType, Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
		WHERE 
			IsValidCustomer = 1
			AND DateID = CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)
			AND InstrumentID IN (
				SELECT InstrumentID
				FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
				WHERE DateID = CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
				GROUP BY InstrumentID
			)
	) AS Filtered
	GROUP BY Instrument, InstrumentType
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
	Amount FOR Metric IN (
		Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
	)
) AS unpvt

UNION ALL 

SELECT 
	'CurrentMonth' AS [Period],
	Instrument,
	InstrumentType,
	Metric,
	Amount
FROM 
(
	SELECT 
		Instrument,
		InstrumentType,
		SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
		SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
		SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
		SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
		SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
		SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
		SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
		SUM(VolumeOnOpen) AS VolumeOnOpen,
		SUM(VolumeOnClose) AS VolumeOnClose
	FROM 
	(
		SELECT Instrument, InstrumentType, Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
		WHERE 
			IsValidCustomer = 1
			AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST(DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, getdate()-1), 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
			AND InstrumentID IN (
				SELECT InstrumentID
				FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
				WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST(DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, getdate()-1), 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
				GROUP BY InstrumentID
			)
	) AS Filtered
	GROUP BY Instrument, InstrumentType
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
	Amount FOR Metric IN (
		Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
	)
) AS unpvt

UNION ALL 

SELECT 
	'PreviousMonthSameTime' AS [Period],
	Instrument,
	InstrumentType,
	Metric,
	Amount
FROM 
(
	SELECT 
		Instrument,
		InstrumentType,
		SUM(Commissions) AS Commissions,
		SUM(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
		SUM(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
		SUM(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
		SUM(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
		SUM(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
		SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
		SUM(VolumeOnOpen) AS VolumeOnOpen,
		SUM(VolumeOnClose) AS VolumeOnClose
	FROM 
	(
		SELECT Instrument, InstrumentType, Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
		WHERE 
			IsValidCustomer = 1
			AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST( DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, getdate()-1) - 1, 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(dateadd(MONTH,-1,getdate()-1)  AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
			AND InstrumentID IN (
				SELECT InstrumentID
				FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg
				WHERE DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST( DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, getdate()-1) - 1, 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(dateadd(MONTH,-1,getdate()-1)  AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)
				GROUP BY InstrumentID
			)
	) AS Filtered
	GROUP BY Instrument, InstrumentType
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
	Amount FOR Metric IN (
		Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
	)
) AS unpvt

UNION ALL 

SELECT a.[Period]
	 , a.Instrument
	 , a.InstrumentType
	 , a.Metric
	 , avg(a.Amount) AS Amount
FROM 
(
	SELECT 
		'SameDay8Weeks' AS [Period],
		Instrument,
		InstrumentType,
		DateID,
		Metric,
		Amount
	FROM 
	(
		SELECT 
			Instrument,
			InstrumentType,
			DateID,
			sum(Commissions) AS Commissions,
			sum(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
			sum(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
			sum(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
			sum(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
			sum(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
			SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
			SUM(VolumeOnOpen) AS VolumeOnOpen,
			SUM(VolumeOnClose) AS VolumeOnClose
		FROM 
		(
			SELECT ia.*
			FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg ia 
			WHERE 
				IsValidCustomer = 1
				AND ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, ia.FullDate) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1 = ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, GETDATE() - 1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1
				AND DATEDIFF(WEEK, ia.FullDate, GETDATE() - 1) <= 8
				AND DATEDIFF(WEEK, ia.FullDate, GETDATE() - 1) > 0			
				AND InstrumentID IN (
					SELECT InstrumentID
					FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg ia
					WHERE ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, ia.FullDate) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1 = ((DATEPART(WEEKDAY, getdate()-1) + @@DATEFIRST - 1) % 7) + 1 AND DATEDIFF (WEEK, ia.FullDate, getdate()-1) <= 8 
					GROUP BY InstrumentID
				)
		) AS Filtered
		GROUP BY Instrument, InstrumentType, Filtered.DateID
	) AS Aggregated
	UNPIVOT
	(
		Amount FOR Metric IN (
			Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
		)
	) AS unpvt
) a
GROUP BY a.Period, a.Instrument, a.InstrumentType, a.Metric

UNION ALL 

SELECT 
	'CurrentYear' AS [Period],
	Instrument,
	InstrumentType,
	Metric,
	Amount
FROM 
(
	SELECT 
		Instrument,
		InstrumentType,
		DateID,
		sum(Commissions) AS Commissions,
		sum(FullCommissions) AS FullCommissions,
		sum(RollOverFee) AS RollOverFee,
		sum(TicketFee) AS TicketFee,
		sum(TicketFeeByPercent) AS TicketFeeByPercent,
		sum(AdminFee) AS AdminFee,
		SUM(SpotAdjustFee) AS SpotAdjustFee,
		SUM(VolumeOnOpen) AS VolumeOnOpen,
		SUM(VolumeOnClose) AS VolumeOnClose
	FROM 
	(
		SELECT ia.*
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg ia 
		WHERE 
			IsValidCustomer = 1
			AND DateID BETWEEN CAST(FORMAT(CAST(DATEADD(yy, DATEDIFF(yy, 0, getdate()-1), 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)  AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
			AND InstrumentID IN (
				SELECT InstrumentID
				FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg ia
				WHERE ia.DateID between CAST(FORMAT(CAST(DATEADD(yy, DATEDIFF(yy, 0, getdate()-1), 0) AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT)  AND CAST(FORMAT(CAST(getdate()-1 AS DATE),'yyyyMMdd') as INT) 
				GROUP BY InstrumentID
			)
	) AS Filtered
	GROUP BY Instrument, InstrumentType, Filtered.DateID
) AS Aggregated
UNPIVOT
(
	Amount FOR Metric IN (
		Commissions, FullCommissions, RollOverFee, TicketFee, TicketFeeByPercent, AdminFee, SpotAdjustFee, VolumeOnOpen, VolumeOnClose
	)
) AS unpvt

## Downstream calculated fields (in embedded datasources)

### Workbook: Commission Daily Report

#### Datasource: BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg (BI_DB)

- **Avg per Day This Year**

  ```
  sum(if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [Full Date] 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end)
  /
  sum(if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **CFD-Real**

  ```
  IF [Settlement Type ID] = 0 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF [Settlement Type ID] = 1 THEN "REAL"
  ELSEIF [Settlement Type ID] = 2 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 1 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 2 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 4 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 10 THEN "REAL"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 5 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 6 THEN "CFD"
  ELSE "NA"
  END
  ```

- **Club **

  ```
  if [Club] = 'N/A' then 'Bronze' 
  ELSEIF [Club] = 'V.I.P' //or [Club] = 'Diamond' or [Club] = 'Platinum Plus' 
  then 'Platinum'
  else [Club]
  end
  ```

- **Desk**

  ```
  if [Region] = "China" or [Region] = "French" or [Region] = "German" 
  or [Region] = "Italian" or [Region] = "UK" or [Region] = "Spain"
  THEN [Region]
  elseif [Region] = "Spanish" then "Spain"
  ELSEIF [Region] = "Arabic GCC & Other" then "Arabic"
  ELSEIF [Region] = "China & Other Asia" then "China"
  ELSEIF [Region] = "Australia" then "Australia"
  else "ROW"
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Full Commissions]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time RollOverFee**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Roll Over Fee]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Roll Over Fee]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time SDRT**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [RollOverFee_SDRT]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [RollOverFee_SDRT]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time Volume**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) < day(TODAY())
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [TotalVolume]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [TotalVolume]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time Volume Open**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) < day(TODAY())
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Volume On Open]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Volume On Open]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time RollOverFee**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [Roll Over Fee]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time SDRT**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [RollOverFee_SDRT]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time Volume**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [TotalVolume]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time Volume Open**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [Volume On Open]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time**

  ```
  if (month(TODAY()) = 1 and day(TODAY()) = 1 and year(TODAY()) = year([Full Date]) + 2)
     or ((MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) 
      or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today()))) and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today()))
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time RollOverFee**

  ```
  if (MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [Roll Over Fee]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time SDRT**

  ```
  if (MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [RollOverFee_SDRT]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time Volume**

  ```
  if (MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [TotalVolume]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time Volume Open**

  ```
  if (MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [Volume On Open]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Number of Records**

  ```
  1
  ```

- **Same DayWeek **

  ```
  'Last 8 weeks Top20'
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [Full Commissions]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks RollOverFee**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [Roll Over Fee]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks SDRT**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [RollOverFee_SDRT]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks Volume**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [TotalVolume]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks Volume Open**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [Volume On Open]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```

- **This Month**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('month',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) <= [Full Date] then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  'Top20'
  ```

- **TotalVolume**

  ```
  [Volume On Open]+[Volume On Close]
  ```

- **VarSpread %**

  ```
  [VarSpreads]/sum([Full Commissions])
  ```

- **VarSpreads**

  ```
  sum([Full Commissions]) - sum([Commissions])
  ```

- **Yestaday**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 1 then [Full Commissions] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 1 then [Full Commissions] else 0

  ```

  end
  ```

- **Yesterday Volume**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 1 then [TotalVolume] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday Volume Open**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 1 then [Volume On Open] else 0
  end
  ```

#### Datasource: BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_LastYear 

- **Last Year**

  ```
  if year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY())) = [Year]+1 then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Number of Records**

  ```
  1
  ```

- **Rank Last Year**

  ```
  RANK( sum([Last Year]),'desc')
  ```

#### Datasource: DailyCommissionReport CID Level

- **2 Days Ago**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 2 then [Commissions] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Accumulated %**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Yesterday])) / TOTAL(SUM([Yesterday]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % Last 8 Weeks**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([SameWeekday Avg8 weeks])) / TOTAL(SUM([SameWeekday Avg8 weeks]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % Last Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Last Month Same Time])) / TOTAL(SUM([Last Month Same Time]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % This Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([This Month])) / TOTAL(SUM([This Month]))
  ```

- **Avg 8 Last Weeks Groups **

  ```
  if [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 200 then 200
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 300 then 300
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 400 then 400
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] >= 5000 then 5001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg Day This Year**

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **Avg Last 8 Weeks Filter**

  ```
  if [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg per Day This Year**

  ```
  sum(if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [Full Date] 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end)
  /
  sum(if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **check**

  ```
  if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Club **

  ```
  if [Club] = 'N/A' then 'Bronze' else [Club]
  end
  ```

- **Contribution to Comm.**

  ```
  if [Accumulated %] < 0.1 then '10% of Comm' 
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.2 then '20% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.3 then '30% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.4 then '40% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.5 then '50% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.99 then '99% of Comm'
  else '100% of Comm'
  end
  ```

  ```
  if [Last Month Same Time] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

  ```

  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  ```

### Workbook: Commission Daily Report - test

#### Datasource: BI_DB_DailyCommisionReport_Instrument_Agg (BI_DB)

- **Avg per Day This Year**

  ```
  sum(if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [Full Date] 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end)
  /
  sum(if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **CFD-Real**

  ```
  IF [Settlement Type ID] = 0 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF [Settlement Type ID] = 1 THEN "REAL"
  ELSEIF [Settlement Type ID] = 2 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 1 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 2 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 4 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 10 THEN "REAL"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 5 THEN "CFD"
  ELSEIF ISNULL([Settlement Type ID]) AND [Instrument Type ID] = 6 THEN "CFD"
  ELSE "NA"
  END
  ```

- **Club **

  ```
  if [Club] = 'N/A' then 'Bronze' 
  ELSEIF [Club] = 'V.I.P' //or [Club] = 'Diamond' or [Club] = 'Platinum Plus' 
  then 'Platinum'
  else [Club]
  end
  ```

- **Desk**

  ```
  if [Region] = "China" or [Region] = "French" or [Region] = "German" 
  or [Region] = "Italian" or [Region] = "UK" or [Region] = "Spain"
  THEN [Region]
  elseif [Region] = "Spanish" then "Spain"
  ELSEIF [Region] = "Arabic GCC & Other" then "Arabic"
  ELSEIF [Region] = "China & Other Asia" then "China"
  ELSEIF [Region] = "Australia" then "Australia"
  else "ROW"
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Full Commissions]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time RollOverFee**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Roll Over Fee]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Roll Over Fee]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time Volume**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) < day(TODAY())
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [TotalVolume]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [TotalVolume]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time Volume Open**

  ```
  if month(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY())) = 1 
      and day([Full Date]) < day(TODAY())
      and MONTH([Full Date]) = 12 
      and year([Full Date])+1 = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Volume On Open]
  ELSEIF  
      day([Full Date]) <= day(dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and MONTH([Full Date])+1 = month(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
      and year([Full Date]) = year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))
  THEN [Volume On Open]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  ```

  then [Roll Over Fee]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time**

  ```
  if (month(TODAY()) = 1 and day(TODAY()) = 1 and year(TODAY()) = year([Full Date]) + 2)
     or ((MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) 
      or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today()))) and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today()))
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  'Top20'
  ```

- **This Year Filter**

  ```
  if [This Year] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Year Groups**

  ```
  if [This Year] < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF [This Year] < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF [This Year] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [This Year] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [This Year] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [This Year] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [This Year] < 10000 then 10000
  ELSEIF  [This Year] < 50000 then 50000
  ELSEIF  [This Year] < 100000 then 100000
  ELSEIF  [This Year] >= 100000 then 100001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[FullDate],TODAY()) = 1 then [Commissions] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Yesterday **

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

#### Datasource: DailyCommisionReport CID Week Level

- **Accumulated % Last Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Last Week])) / TOTAL(SUM([Last Week]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % This Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([This Week])) / TOTAL(SUM([This Week]))
  ```

- **Avg 8 Last Weeks Groups **

  ```
  if [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 200 then 200
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 300 then 300
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 400 then 400
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [Calculation_474566850693619712] >= 5000 then 5001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg Day This Year**

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **Avg Last 8 Weeks Filter**

  ```
  if [Calculation_474566850693619712] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **check**

  ```
  if YEAR([FullDate]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[FullDate]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[FullDate]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Club **

  ```
  if [Club] = 'N/A' then 'Bronze' else [Club]
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Filter**

  ```
  if [Last Week] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Groups**

  ```
  if [Last Week] < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF [Last Week] < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF [Last Week] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] < 2000 then 2000
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] < 10000 then 10000
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] < 20000 then 20000
  ELSEIF  [Last Week] >= 20000 then 20001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Week**

  ```
  if [Week]+1=DATEPART('week',today()) + year(today()) *100
  then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week **

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time- Old**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [FullDate] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [FullDate]
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time**

  ```
  if (MONTH([FullDate]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([FullDate]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([FullDate])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([FullDate])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Number of Records**

  ```
  1
  ```

- **Rank**

  ```
  RANK( sum([This Week]),'desc')
  ```

- **Rank Last Week**

  ```
  RANK( sum([Last Week]),'desc')
  ```

- **Same DayWeek **

  ```
  'Last 8 weeks Top20'
  ```

- **Test**

  ```
  [This Month Groups]
  ```

- **This Month Groups**

  ```
  if [This Week] < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF [This Week] < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF [This Week] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [This Week] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [This Week] < 1000 then 1000

  ELSEIF  [This Week] < 10000 then 10000
  ELSEIF  [This Week] < 20000 then 20000
  ELSEIF  [This Week] >= 20000 then 20001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Quarter**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('quarter',TODAY()) <= [FullDate] then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Week**

  ```
  if DATEPART('week',DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY())) + year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))*100 = [Week] then [Full Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Week **

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **This Week Commission in risk**

  ```
  if DATEPART('week',DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY())) + year(DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY()))*100 = [Week] then CommissionInRisk
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Week Filter**

  ```
  if [This Week] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Week old**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,TODAY())) <= [FullDate] then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **This Year**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [FullDate] then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  ```
  if datediff('day',[FullDate],TODAY()) = 1 then [Commissions] else 0
  end

#### Datasource: DailyCommissionReport CID Level

- **2 Days Ago**

  ```
  if datediff('day',[Full Date],TODAY()) = 2 then [Commissions] else 0
  end
  ```

- **Accumulated %**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Yesterday])) / TOTAL(SUM([Yesterday]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % Last 8 Weeks**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([SameWeekday Avg8 weeks])) / TOTAL(SUM([SameWeekday Avg8 weeks]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % Last Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([Last Month Same Time])) / TOTAL(SUM([Last Month Same Time]))
  ```

- **Accumulated % This Month**

  ```
  RUNNING_SUM(SUM([This Month])) / TOTAL(SUM([This Month]))
  ```

- **Avg 8 Last Weeks Groups **

  ```
  if [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 200 then 200
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 300 then 300
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 400 then 400
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] >= 5000 then 5001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg Day This Year**

  ```
  'Top20'
  ```

- **Avg Last 8 Weeks Filter**

  ```
  if [SameWeekday Avg8 weeks] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Avg per Day This Year**

  ```
  sum(if DATETRUNC('year',TODAY()) <= [Full Date] 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end)
  /
  sum(if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end)
  ```

- **check**

  ```
  if YEAR([Full Date]) = YEAR(TODAY()) 
  and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 6 and DATEPART('weekday',[Full Date]) != 7
  then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **Club **

  ```
  if [Club] = 'N/A' then 'Bronze' else [Club]
  end
  ```

- **Contribution to Comm.**

  ```
  if [Accumulated %] < 0.1 then '10% of Comm' 
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.2 then '20% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.3 then '30% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.4 then '40% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.5 then '50% of Comm'
  ELSEIF [Accumulated %] < 0.99 then '99% of Comm'
  else '100% of Comm'
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Filter**

  ```
  if [Last Month Same Time] > 0 then 1 else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time**

  ```
  if day([Full Date])<day(today()) and MONTH([Full Date])+1=MONTH(today()) and year([Full Date]) = year(TODAY())
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Month Same Time Groups**

  ```
  if [Last Month Same Time] < 1 then 1
  ELSEIF [Last Month Same Time] < 10 then 10
  ELSEIF [Last Month Same Time] < 100 then 100
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 500 then 500
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 1000 then 1000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 2000 then 2000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 5000 then 5000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 10000 then 10000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] < 20000 then 20000
  ELSEIF  [Last Month Same Time] >= 20000 then 20001
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Week Same Time**

  ```
  if DATETRUNC('week',DATEADD('day',-1,dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()))) <= [Full Date] 
  and dateadd('day',-7,TODAY()) > [Full Date]
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

- **Last Year Same**

  ```
  'Time Top20'
  ```

- **Last Year Same Time**

  ```
  if (MONTH([Full Date]) < MONTH(TODAY()) or (MONTH([Full Date]) = MONTH(TODAY()) and DAY([Full Date])<DAY(today())))
  and YEAR([Full Date])+1=YEAR(today())
  then [Commissions]
  else 0
  end
  ```

  1

  ```

- **Same DayWeek **

  ```
  'Last 8 weeks Top20'
  ```

- **SameWeekday Avg8 weeks**

  ```
  if datepart('weekday',[Full Date])=datepart('weekday',dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))>0 
  and datediff('week',[Full Date],dateadd('day',-1,TODAY()))<=8 
  then [Commissions]/8 else 0 
  end
  ```
